<h3>Integrated Project Management Software - for Desktop, Tablet and Smartphone</h3> <hr/> </div> <div class="column col-xs-12 col-sm-7">
<p>The <a href="http://www.inloox.com/project-management-software/" target="_self">project management software</a> <b>InLoox </b>operates within <b>Microsoft Outlook® and the Web</b>, simplifying and combining the organization of <b>projects, documents, resources</b> and <b>budgets</b>. InLoox provides highly effective support for everyday standard business processes.</p><p>InLoox is a full-featured business management software product that helps you save time on <b>project planning, processing, tracking, scheduling, </b><b><a href="http://www.inloox.com/resource-management-software/" target="_self">resource management</a> </b>and completing your project successfully. Old <a href="http://www.inloox.com/project-planning-software/" target="_self">project planning software</a> and management software tools put the burden of creating and updating project plans on the manager's shoulders. InLoox offers an online project planning software solution at a fraction of the costs of enterprise project management suites.</p><p>InLoox makes your project planning and management quicker and easier for team members. It is the project tracking and <b>project management software</b> you need to make collaboration among the teams and team members effective.</p><p>InLoox project management software can improve the quality and speed of your company's client interactions, InLoox's powerful reporting skills and features such as workflow notifications facilitate improved project risk management software solution for people separated by vast distances and time-zones. It can also be the perfect <a href="http://www.inloox.com/project-tracking-software/" target="_self">time tracking</a> and project planning software tool for team members working in one office as well as for geographically dispersed teams. With InLoox, your company will be equipped to complete each project on time and in budget.</p> </div> <div class="column col-xs-12 col-sm-5">
<div class="row">
